                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>

(S.) When it is made determinate without the article <foreign lang="ar">ال</foreign>, [as] in the name <foreign lang="ar">عَبْدُ شَمْسَ</foreign>, meaning <hi rend="ital">The Servant of the Sun,</hi> (Msb, K,) i. e., of this luminous object, (Msb,) the <foreign lang="ar">شمس</foreign> of heaven, because they used to worship it, (K,) it is imperfectly decl., (Aboo- 'Alee, Msb, K,) because it is determinate and of the fem. gender, (Aboo-'Alee, K,) or because it is a proper name and of the fem. gender and altered from <foreign lang="ar">الشَّمْس</foreign>: (Msb:) and a poet says, <quote>

                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> A horse <hi rend="ital">that refuses to be ridden</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mounted;</hi> (S, K;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23003-1" target="شَامِسٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n23006"/></foreign>: (K:) or <hi rend="ital">that takes fright and breaks loose and runs away, refusing to be ridden, by reason of the vehemence of his force of resistance and his sharpness of temper, so that he will not remain still:</hi> (TA: [see 1:]) or <hi rend="ital">that will hardly remain still:</hi> (A:) or <hi rend="ital">that rebels against his rider:</hi> (Msb:) or <hi rend="ital">that refuses to be ridden</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mounted, and will hardly remain still:</hi> (Mgh:) also applied to a she-camel: (TA:) <foreign lang="ar">شَمُوصٌ</foreign>, with <foreign lang="ar">ص</foreign>, applied to a horse is not allowable: (Msb:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">شُمُسٌ</foreign> (A, Mgh, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">شُمْسٌ</foreign>. (K.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [Hence,] <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  A woman <hi rend="ital">who abstains from looking at men, and from exciting their desire;</hi> as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23003-2" target="شَامِسَةٌ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>: pl. of the former, <foreign lang="ar">شُمُسٌ</foreign>; and of the latter, [<foreign lang="ar">شَوَامِسُ</foreign> and] <foreign lang="ar">شُمُوسٌ</foreign>. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  Hence also, (Msb,) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  A man <hi rend="ital">refractory, untractable, perverse, stubborn,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">obstinate, in disposition:</hi> (S, Msb, TA:) and a man <hi rend="ital">hard, harsh,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">illnatured, in his enmity, vehement in contrariousness to him who opposes him:</hi> (TA:) <foreign lang="ar">شَمُوصٌ</foreign> [with <foreign lang="ar">ص</foreign>] is not allowable. (S.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  [Hence too,] <foreign lang="ar">الشَّمُوسُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">Wine:</hi> (AHn, K:) because it overcomes, and runs away with, its drinker, like the horse to which this epithet is applied.
